{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+T\+O\+K\+E\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+I\+R\+ED = 109\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

The Token expired due to one of the following reasons\+: 
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Authorized Timestamp expired\+: The timestamp is represented by the number of seconds elapsed since 1/1/1970. The user can use the Token to access the Agora service within five minutes after the Token is generated. If the user does not access the Agora service after five minutes, this Token will no longer be valid. 
\item Call Expiration Timestamp expired\+: The timestamp indicates the exact time when a user can no longer use the Agora service (for example, when a user is forced to leave an ongoing call). When the value is set for the Call Expiration Timestamp, it does not mean that the Dynamic Key will be expired, but that the user will be kicked out of the channel.$<$/il$>$
\end{DoxyEnumerate}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_ad1ce36f4a38c1c277ecf4de9776805b3}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_ad1ce36f4a38c1c277ecf4de9776805b3}}

\index{io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}!SINGING\_BEAUTIFIER@{SINGING\_BEAUTIFIER}}
\index{SINGING\_BEAUTIFIER@{SINGING\_BEAUTIFIER}!io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SINGING\_BEAUTIFIER}{SINGING\_BEAUTIFIER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+S\+I\+N\+G\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+B\+E\+A\+U\+T\+I\+F\+I\+ER = 0x01020100\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Singing beautifier effect.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_a5a866fbb28c34fc38c3f600f78d61e73}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset(\+S\+I\+N\+G\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+B\+E\+A\+U\+T\+I\+F\+I\+E\+R)}}, you can beautify a male-\/sounding voice and add a reverberation effect that sounds like singing in a small room. Agora recommends not using {\ttfamily set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset(\+S\+I\+N\+G\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+B\+E\+A\+U\+T\+I\+F\+I\+E\+R)} to process a female-\/sounding voice; otherwise, you may experience vocal distortion.
\item If you call \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af712699445c8ff8118f5d1027dc636ca}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters(\+S\+I\+N\+G\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+B\+E\+A\+U\+T\+I\+F\+I\+E\+R, param1, param2)}}, you can beautify a male-\/ or female-\/sounding voice and add a reverberation effect.
\end{DoxyItemize}

A 3D voice effect that makes the voice appear to be moving around the user. The default cycle period of the 3D voice effect is 10 seconds. To change the cycle period, call \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_aaf70d13931b9a2194cd96284b37dc071}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters\} after this method. Call  Rtc\+Engine\#set\+Audio\+Profile set\+Audio\+Profile\} and set the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(3)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before setting this enumerator; otherwise, the enumerator setting does not take effectIf the 3D voice effect is enabled, users need to use stereo audio playback devices to hear the anticipated voice effect. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a3d1326e24c673e1d829af8e7a0828011}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a3d1326e24c673e1d829af8e7a0828011}}

virtual suround sound.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Agora recommends using this enumerator to process virtual suround sound; otherwise, you may not hear the anticipated voice effect.
\item To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling set\+Audio\+Profile and setting the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y(4)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before setting this enumerator. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

High Priority, if you set a user with high priority, then streams of this user will have high priority than streams of other users with normal default priority. i.\+e., the S\+DK will take priority into account when deciding which user\textquotesingle{}s stream need to fallback when network congestion occurs. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_ac87dc70bb144efc48cdaaddf1b3c47cf}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_ac87dc70bb144efc48cdaaddf1b3c47cf}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+R\+T\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+S\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+V\+E\+R\+I\+NG = 3\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

3\+: The R\+T\+MP streaming is recovering. When exceptions occur to the C\+DN, or the streaming is interrupted, the S\+DK tries to resume R\+T\+MP streaming and reports this state.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the S\+DK successfully resumes the streaming, {\ttfamily R\+T\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+S\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+U\+N\+N\+I\+N\+G(2)} is reported.
\item If the streaming does not resume within 60 seconds or server errors occur, {\ttfamily R\+T\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+S\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+R\+E(4)} is reported. You can also reconnect to the server by calling {\ttfamily remove\+Publish\+Stream\+Url} and {\ttfamily add\+Publish\+Stream\+Url}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_ac9189b30b58dda24d36ea9d01c7c0380}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_ac9189b30b58dda24d36ea9d01c7c0380}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CONNECTION\_STATE\_DISCONNECTED}{CONNECTION\_STATE\_DISCONNECTED}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+ED = 1\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

1\+: The S\+DK is disconnected from Agora edge server. 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This is the initial state before calling the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method. 
\item The S\+DK also enters this state when the app calls the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}{leave\+Channel}} method. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_af01f606596669168030decf672aaa154}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_af01f606596669168030decf672aaa154}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}!CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTING@{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTING}}
\index{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTING@{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTING}!io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTING}{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTING}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+NG = 2\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

2\+: The S\+DK is connecting to Agora edge server. 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When the app calls the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method, the S\+DK starts to establish a connection to the specified channel, triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_acf3ab9feae0d9a6001da31e95363aa22}{on\+Connection\+State\+Changed}} callback, and switches to the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_af01f606596669168030decf672aaa154}{C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+NG\} state. }}When a user successfully joins a channel, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_acf3ab9feae0d9a6001da31e95363aa22}{on\+Connection\+State\+Changed\} callback and switches to the  Constants\#\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+ED C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+ED\} state. }}After the S\+DK joins the channel and when it finishes initializing the media engine, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a25a599788cbb7d9b97b9f67747c17243}{on\+Join\+Channel\+Success}} callback. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a8738a89b8c423ecba13592e53f6d5503}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a8738a89b8c423ecba13592e53f6d5503}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}!CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTED@{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTED}}
\index{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTED@{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTED}!io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTED}{CONNECTION\_STATE\_CONNECTED}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+ED = 3\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

3\+: The S\+DK is connected to Agora edge server and has joined a channel. You can now publish or subscribe to a media stream in the channel. If the connection to the channel is lost because, for example, the network is down or switched, the S\+DK triggers\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ae295db0a95c7d6409b19b00dfef9ed20}{on\+Connection\+Interrupted}} (deprecated) callback. 
\item The \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_acf3ab9feae0d9a6001da31e95363aa22}{on\+Connection\+State\+Changed}} callback, and switches to the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a405f64ad7916414a06af2642b7e73dbb}{C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+NG\} state. }} 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a405f64ad7916414a06af2642b7e73dbb}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a405f64ad7916414a06af2642b7e73dbb}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}!CONNECTION\_STATE\_RECONNECTING@{CONNECTION\_STATE\_RECONNECTING}}
\index{CONNECTION\_STATE\_RECONNECTING@{CONNECTION\_STATE\_RECONNECTING}!io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CONNECTION\_STATE\_RECONNECTING}{CONNECTION\_STATE\_RECONNECTING}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+NG = 4\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

4\+: The S\+DK keeps rejoining the channel after being disconnected from a joined channel because of network issues. 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the S\+DK cannot join the channel within 10 seconds after being disconnected from Agora edge server, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a3c40049545254582b454eea461b166f4}{on\+Connection\+Lost\} (deprecated) callback, stays in the  Constants\#\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+NG C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+NG\} state, and keeps rejoining the channel. }}If the S\+DK fails to rejoin the channel 20 minutes after being disconnected from Agora edge server, the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_acf3ab9feae0d9a6001da31e95363aa22}{on\+Connection\+State\+Changed\} callback, switches to the  Constants\#\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED\} state, and stops rejoining the channel. }} 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a4c9d66474e974fa5b22ecf64f7126fa5}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_a4c9d66474e974fa5b22ecf64f7126fa5}} 
\index{io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}!CONNECTION\_STATE\_FAILED@{CONNECTION\_STATE\_FAILED}}
\index{CONNECTION\_STATE\_FAILED@{CONNECTION\_STATE\_FAILED}!io.agora.rtc2.Constants@{io.agora.rtc2.Constants}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CONNECTION\_STATE\_FAILED}{CONNECTION\_STATE\_FAILED}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED = 5\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

5\+: The S\+DK fails to connect to Agora edge server or join the channel. You must call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_af3fe5d61a9ca8db36b56432273d02307}{leave\+Channel}} method to leave this state and call the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method again to rejoin the channel. If the S\+DK is banned from joining the channel by the Agora server (through the R\+E\+S\+Tful A\+PI), the S\+DK triggers the \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a3699579c7e341ea19e185b967748ddd4}{on\+Connection\+Banned\} and \{ I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler\#on\+Connection\+State\+Changed on\+Connection\+State\+Changed\} callbacks. }}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_abb606ad5c57343a839ea09b8b34546c1}\label{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_constants_abb606ad5c57343a839ea09b8b34546c1}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily final int io.\+agora.\+rtc2.\+Constants.\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+C\+R\+E\+E\+N\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+T\+U\+R\+E\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+S\+T\+E\+M\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED = 3\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

3\+: Due to system limitations, system audio cannot be captured on systems earlier than Android 10 (that is, A\+PI level 29). The S\+DK reports this error when you call \{\mbox{\hyperlink{classio_1_1agora_1_1rtc2_1_1_rtc_engine_abf71be90a0e958aee09558be1aa225aa}{start\+Screen\+Capture\} and set {\ttfamily capture\+Audio} as {\ttfamily true} on systems later than Android 5 (A\+PI level 21) and earlier than Android 10 (A\+PI level 29).  v3.\+7.\+0 }}
